why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班的教育 , 在這段時間裡 , 這些男女都學會了閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀 , 通過北約組織合作 , 通過和私人機構合作 , 通過與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過20萬阿富汗安全部隊 , 基本上可以讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你可以在阿富汗閱讀和寫作時 , 你通常會在口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們很驕傲地拿下那筆 , 放進他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這也為國際整合了50個國家共同投入任務各國間的國際安全部門這些發展部門私人和公共產業致力於此
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們對抗技能 , 但我認為 , 開放式安全意味著用能夠創造更持久的安全方式來做連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	所謂的舒適感
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫默西的姊妹船
they are hospital ships .	它們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 安慰號在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	一般而言 , 他們會進行400 , 000個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是嚴格看待軍隊的 , 而是結合了人道主義組織:希望、專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	國際間的醫生也出場了 。
they're all part of this .	它們都是這現象的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	給你們一個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 8歲 , 跟他媽媽走了兩天來到安慰號的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他靈光乍現時 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	" 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 "
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以40萬的病患治療 , 這個私人與安全部隊合作的私人公共合作 , 你就會開始看到以截然不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	在這裡你看到棒球選手 ,
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩名美國陸軍部隊的士兵嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這群小男孩兩邊的小男孩 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 , 我們已經在那裡探討了大聯盟棒球聯賽 , 國務院設立了外交部 , 軍事棒球員 , 他們是真正的戰士 , 但他們參與了這個任務 , 他們在美國和加勒比海各地開了診所 , 開了診所 , 在宏都拉斯和加勒比 , 開了安全帶 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展示了關于健身和生活的榜樣 , 我主張協助為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這個合作的另一方面是災難救援 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機 , 參與了2004年的海嘯 , 殺死了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在每場重大災難中 , 2004年海嘯二十五萬人死亡 , 巴基斯坦的喀什米里地震 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死於海地地震 , 大約有30萬人死於海地震 , 還有最近發生在日本嚴重的地震海嘯雙重打擊日本和它的核產業 。 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際組織、跨部門合作、私人協會 , 和這種自然的安全合作 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些都是開放式安全理念的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 藉由像這樣的事 ,
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿道德 , 這些一定是通訊的海上航線 , 或者這些也許是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不是 。 這是twitter公司所繪製的世界地圖 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地緣 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是綜合體 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是個完美的驅動人口調查 , 世界上六大國家的排名順序如下:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們會想拿到這些網子 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 它是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦待了一陣子我跟你們說我在臉書上 , 朋友
got a little laugh from the audience .	得到觀眾的小笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇ap的文章 , 在電線上執行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被世界上兩個地方接起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約艦隊司令需要好友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百個臉書朋友的請求 , 來自印尼人和芬恩斯 , 大部分都會說: 「 司機 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 哦 , 順帶一提 , nato是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這是我們如何移動訊息 , 將訊息傳送出去 , 就是我們如何連結國際、跨部門、私人作業 , 還有這些社群網路 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我用一個嚴肅的方式來說明 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭護衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正站在helmand的立場 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要 , 競爭的軍事力量 , 能夠創造真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們是誰的核心 , 我們所做的 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的東西 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但你知道 , 生活並不是一個隨機的開關
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支隊伍 , 不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在戰鬥中 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我主張生命是一種表面的表面
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須調整一下 , 就在我看來 , 我們在21世紀是如何創造安全的時候 , 會有時候 , 我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中 , 真正的戰爭和危機中 , 應用強硬的力量 , 但 , 如同我們今天談過的 , 我們的軍隊能夠參與 , 創造21世紀的安全、國際、跨部門、私人、公共和公共安全 , 以競爭力連結在一起 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我想說 , 我們今天早些時候聽到維基百科了 。 我經常使用維基百科查詢事實 , 正如你們所有人所理解的 , 維基百科不是靠12個聰明的人把自己關在一個房間裡寫文章而產生的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每一天都有數百萬人在使用那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 對於基本的重點 , 我們沒有人能像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 我們沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:一個人人都可以自由地分享所有知識的總和 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 公私力量 , 策略性溝通 , 一同合作 , 在這個21世紀 , 我們能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
